From +18329730364 to you
2016/10/06 22:33:35
Texas is a permissive driver state, meaning, as long as you give someone permission to drive your car, your insurance policy will cover that driver.  If someone uses your car without your permission, such as a car thief, then your insurance policy will not cover that driver.  Therefore, it typically does not matter whether the driver of the car is listed on the insurance policy as long as they had permission to drive from the owner.  The exception to this general rule is when the insurance company has specifically excluded a particular person from driving the car in the policy.  This situation often occurs with families who have young teenage children.  Teenagers are seen as risky and often times insurance companies will require their insureds to specifically exclude their teenage children as covered persons.
